                    <div class="pera">
                                                                                    <p> Drafted <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/draft/chl-import-draft/2002">2002, 1 #15 overall by Medicine Hat Tigers</a> in the CHL Import Draft </p>
                                                    
                        
                        
                                                                                    <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/1674/belarus"> Belarus </a> </p>
                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/17166/hk-sochi"> HK Sochi </a> </p>
                                                    
                                                    <p><b>Career transactions</b><br>
- 2013-06-13 • Signed to a one-year contract extension by Traktor Chelyabinsk<br>
- 2012-09-14 • Signed to a one-year contract by Traktor Chelyabinsk<br>
- 2012-02-27 • Traded to the Nashville Predators for a 2013 2nd round pick (<a href="player.php?player=28436">Jacob de la Rose</a>) & a conditional 2013 5th round pick<br>
- 2011-06-09 • Re-signed to a one-year contract by the Montréal Canadiens<br>
- 2008-07-01 • Re-signed to a three-year contract by the Montréal Canadiens<br>
- 2004-08-10 • Re-signed to a three-year contract by the Montréal Canadiens<br></p>
